          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

          width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

v8::MaybeLocal<v8::Value> CallMethodOnFrame(LocalFrame* local_frame,



<span class="line"><!---->v8::MaybeLocal&lt;v8::Value&gt; CallMethodOnFrame(LocalFrame* local_frame,<!----></span>



<br>





                                            const String& object_name,



<span class="line"><!---->                                            const String&amp; object_name,<!----></span>



<br>





                                            const String& method_name,



<span class="line"><!---->                                            const String&amp; method_name,<!----></span>



<br>





                                            base::Value::List arguments,



<span class="line"><!---->                                            base::Value::List arguments,<!----></span>



<br>





                                            WebV8ValueConverter* converter) {



<span class="line"><!---->                                            WebV8ValueConverter* converter) {<!----></span>



<br>





  v8::Local<v8::Context> context = MainWorldScriptContext(local_frame);



<span class="line"><!---->  v8::Local&lt;v8::Context&gt; context = MainWorldScriptContext(local_frame);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  v8::Context::Scope context_scope(context);



<span class="line"><!---->  v8::Context::Scope context_scope(context);<!----></span>



<br>





  WTF::Vector<v8::Local<v8::Value>> args;



<span class="line"><!---->  WTF::Vector&lt;v8::Local&lt;v8::Value&gt;&gt; args;<!----></span>



<br>





  for (const auto& argument : arguments) {



<span class="line"><!---->  for (const auto&amp; argument : arguments) {<!----></span>



<br>





    args.push_back(converter->ToV8Value(argument, context));



<span class="line"><!---->    args.push_back(converter-&gt;ToV8Value(argument, context));<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  v8::Local<v8::Value> object;



<span class="line"><!---->  v8::Local&lt;v8::Value&gt; object;<!----></span>



<br>





  v8::Local<v8::Value> method;



<span class="line"><!---->  v8::Local&lt;v8::Value&gt; method;<!----></span>



<br>





  if (!GetProperty(context, context->Global(), object_name).ToLocal(&object) ||



<span class="line"><!---->  if (!GetProperty(context, context-&gt;Global(), object_name).ToLocal(&amp;object) ||<!----></span>



<br>





      !GetProperty(context, object, method_name).ToLocal(&method)) {



<span class="line"><!---->      !GetProperty(context, object, method_name).ToLocal(&amp;method)) {<!----></span>



<br>





    return v8::MaybeLocal<v8::Value>();



<span class="line"><!---->    return v8::MaybeLocal&lt;v8::Value&gt;();<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  CHECK(method->IsFunction());



<span class="line"><!---->  CHECK(method-&gt;IsFunction());<!----></span>



<br>





  return local_frame->DomWindow()



<span class="line"><!---->  return local_frame-&gt;DomWindow()<!----></span>



<br>





      ->GetScriptController()



<span class="line"><!---->      -&gt;GetScriptController()<!----></span>



<br>





      .EvaluateMethodInMainWorld(v8::Local<v8::Function>::Cast(method), object,       // here will cast to v8::Function without check its type



<span class="line"><!---->      .EvaluateMethodInMainWorld(v8::Local&lt;v8::Function&gt;::Cast(method), object,       // here will cast to v8::Function without check its type<!----></span>



<br>





                                 static_cast<int>(args.size()), args.data());



<span class="line"><!---->                                 static_cast&lt;int&gt;(args.size()), args.data());<!----></span>

}

Date: Wed Jan 11 05:55:14 2023



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Jan 11 05:55:14 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[devtools] Ensure that invoked method is an actual v8::Function



<span class="line"><!---->[devtools] Ensure that invoked method is an actual v8::Function<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CallMethodOnFrame invokes a function part of an object which in turn



<span class="line"><!---->CallMethodOnFrame invokes a function part of an object which in turn<!----></span>



<br>





is installed on globalThis. E.g. globalThis['foo'].bar();



<span class="line"><!---->is installed on globalThis. E.g. globalThis['foo'].bar();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CallMethodOnFrame already bails out if 'foo' or 'bar' can't be found,



<span class="line"><!---->CallMethodOnFrame already bails out if 'foo' or 'bar' can't be found,<!----></span>



<br>





but we should also bail out if 'bar' is not an actual function.



<span class="line"><!---->but we should also bail out if 'bar' is not an actual function.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Fixed: 1404704



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1404704" title="V8 type confusion of object as v8::Function in CallMethodOnFrame"><!---->Fixed: 1404704<!----></a>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
